*The last date for deposit for second quarter (Q2) advance tax installment is 15th Sep'22

* You should deposit at least 45% of your projected tax liability

* The advance tax is to be computed after taking the effect of TDS projections say on salary, interest, rent etc

* Pay advance tax by selecting challan 280 while paying tax online through 'e-payment for TIN' website

*If you ignore to deposit advance tax, additional interest is attracted
